==================================================
FILE: ./build_site.py
==================================================
import json
import os
import shutil
import re
from datetime import datetime
from jinja2 import Environment, FileSystemLoader

# --- CONFIGURATION ---
INPUT_DIR = 'input'
DB_DIR = 'db'
OUTPUT_DIR = 'docs'
TEMPLATE_DIR = 'templates'
SITE_URL = "https://saqibkh.github.io/InstructionSets" 

os.makedirs(DB_DIR, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(OUTPUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# --- HELPERS ---
def validate_instruction(inst):
    required = ['mnemonic', 'architecture', 'summary', 'encoding']
    missing = [key for key in required if key not in inst]
    if missing:
        print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è  Warning: {inst.get('mnemonic', 'Unknown')} missing keys: {missing}")
        return False
    return True

def parse_encoding(pattern):
    if not pattern: return []
    if '|' in pattern: return [p.strip() for p in pattern.split('|')]
    if '+' in pattern: return [p.strip() for p in pattern.split('+')]
    return [p.strip() for p in pattern.split()]

def create_linkifier(mnemonic_map):
    sorted_keys = sorted(mnemonic_map.keys(), key=len, reverse=True)
    pattern = re.compile(r'\b(' + '|'.join(re.escape(k) for k in sorted_keys) + r')\b')

    def linkify(text):
        if not text: return ""
        def replace(match):
            m = match.group(0)
            return f'<a href="{mnemonic_map[m]}" class="cross-link">{m}</a>'
        return pattern.sub(replace, text)
    return linkify

# --- CORE LOGIC ---
def load_and_merge_data():
    master_db = {} 
    if os.path.exists(DB_DIR):
        for filename in os.listdir(DB_DIR):
            if filename.endswith('.json'):
                arch_name = filename.replace('.json', '')
                with open(os.path.join(DB_DIR, filename), 'r') as f:
                    master_db[arch_name] = json.load(f)

    if os.path.exists(INPUT_DIR):
        for filename in os.listdir(INPUT_DIR):
            if filename.endswith('.json'):
                filepath = os.path.join(INPUT_DIR, filename)
                with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
                    try:
                        new_data = json.load(f)
                        for inst in new_data.get('instructions', []):
                            if not validate_instruction(inst): continue
                            arch = inst.get('architecture', 'Unknown')
                            if arch not in master_db: master_db[arch] = []
                            exists = any(i['mnemonic'] == inst['mnemonic'] for i in master_db[arch])
                            if not exists:
                                master_db[arch].append(inst)
                                print(f"‚úÖ Added {inst['mnemonic']} to {arch}")
                    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                        print(f"‚ùå Error decoding {filename}: {e}")

    for arch, instructions in master_db.items():
        with open(os.path.join(DB_DIR, f"{arch}.json"), 'w') as f:
            json.dump(instructions, f, indent=2)
    return master_db

def generate_site(master_db):
    env = Environment(loader=FileSystemLoader(TEMPLATE_DIR))
    
    mnemonic_to_url = {}
    search_index = []
    all_pages = []

    for arch, insts in master_db.items():
        for inst in insts:
            clean_name = inst['mnemonic'].lower().replace(' ', '_')
            rel_url = f"{arch.lower()}/{clean_name}/"
            mnemonic_to_url[inst['mnemonic']] = f"../../{rel_url}"
            
            search_index.append({
                "label": f"{inst['mnemonic']} ({arch})",
                "url": rel_url,
                "summary": inst['summary'],
                "arch": arch
            })
            all_pages.append(rel_url)

    linkify = create_linkifier(mnemonic_to_url)

    with open(os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'search.json'), 'w') as f:
        json.dump(search_index, f)

    sitemap_content = ['<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>', '<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">']
    today = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    for page in all_pages:
        sitemap_content.append(f"  <url><loc>{SITE_URL}/{page}</loc><lastmod>{today}</lastmod></url>")
    sitemap_content.append('</urlset>')
    
    with open(os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'sitemap.xml'), 'w') as f:
        f.write('\n'.join(sitemap_content))

    static_src = 'static'
    static_dest = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'static')
    if os.path.exists(static_dest): shutil.rmtree(static_dest)
    if os.path.exists(static_src): shutil.copytree(static_src, static_dest)

    template_detail = env.get_template('instruction_detail.html')
    template_summary = env.get_template('arch_summary.html')
    template_index = env.get_template('index.html')

    # HOMEPAGE
    arch_counts = {arch: len(insts) for arch, insts in master_db.items()}
    with open(os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'index.html'), 'w') as f:
        f.write(template_index.render(
            architectures=list(master_db.keys()), 
            counts=arch_counts,
            root="."
        ))

    for arch, instructions in master_db.items():
        sorted_insts = sorted(instructions, key=lambda x: x['mnemonic'])
        
        # --- NEW: Enhanced Pre-processing ---
        for inst in instructions:
            # 1. Parse Encoding with cleanup
            if 'encoding' in inst and 'binary_pattern' in inst['encoding']:
                raw_parts = parse_encoding(inst['encoding']['binary_pattern'])
                inst['encoding']['visual_parts'] = []
                for p in raw_parts:
                    # Clean "imm[11:0]" -> "imm" for matching
                    clean_name = p.split('[')[0].strip()
                    inst['encoding']['visual_parts'].append({
                        'raw': p, 
                        'clean': clean_name
                    })
            
            # 2. Cross-Link
            inst['linked_summary'] = linkify(inst['summary'])
            inst['linked_pseudocode'] = linkify(inst.get('pseudocode', ''))

        # ARCH SUMMARY
        arch_dir = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, arch.lower())
        os.makedirs(arch_dir, exist_ok=True)
        with open(os.path.join(arch_dir, 'index.html'), 'w') as f:
            f.write(template_summary.render(
                arch=arch, 
                instructions=sorted_insts,
                root=".."
            ))
        
        # DETAIL PAGES
        for inst in instructions:
            safe_name = inst['mnemonic'].lower().replace(' ', '_')
            inst_dir = os.path.join(arch_dir, safe_name)
            os.makedirs(inst_dir, exist_ok=True)
            
            with open(os.path.join(inst_dir, 'index.html'), 'w') as f:
                f.write(template_detail.render(
                    instruction=inst,
                    sidebar_nav=sorted_insts,
                    current_page=inst['mnemonic'],
                    root="../.."
                ))

    print("üöÄ Website generation complete!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("Scanning for new data...")
    db = load_and_merge_data()
    print("Building HTML...")
    generate_site(db)

<script>
    // Bridge the hero input to the main search logic if present
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        const heroInput = document.getElementById('hero-search');
        const heroResults = document.getElementById('hero-results');
        const mainInput = document.getElementById('search-input'); // The nav bar input
        
        // Hide nav bar input on homepage to avoid clutter
        if(mainInput && window.innerWidth > 768) {
             mainInput.closest('.search-wrapper').style.visibility = 'hidden';
        }

        // Reuse the logic by dispatching events or simple duplication
        // For simplicity in this mega-update, I'll let search.js handle the Nav one, 
        // and copy the minimal fetch logic here for the Hero one to ensure it works 100%
        
        let searchIndex = [];
        fetch('search.json')
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => searchIndex = data);

        heroInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
            heroResults.innerHTML = '';
            if (query.length < 2) { heroResults.style.display = 'none'; return; }

            const terms = query.split(" ");
            const results = searchIndex.filter(item => {
                const text = (item.label + " " + item.summary).toLowerCase();
                return terms.every(term => text.includes(term));
            });

            if (results.length > 0) {
                heroResults.style.display = 'block';
                results.slice(0, 8).forEach(result => {
                    const div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.className = 'search-result-item';
                    div.innerHTML = `<a href="${result.url}"><div class="result-title">${result.label}</div><div class="result-summary">${result.summary}</div></a>`;
                    heroResults.appendChild(div);
                });
            } else { heroResults.style.display = 'none'; }
        });
        
        // Keyboard shortcut focuses Hero input on Homepage
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'k') {
                e.preventDefault();
                heroInput.focus();
            }
        });
    });
</script>

        <p>Generated automatically from JSON definitions. <a href="./sitemap.xml" style="color: var(--accent);">Sitemap</a></p>

                AUIPC

            <h1 class="mono" style="font-size: 3rem; margin-top: 10px;">AUIPC</h1>
            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Add Upper Immediate to PC</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                AUIPC rd, imm
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Adds a 20-bit upper immediate to the Program Counter.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            R[rd] = PC + (imm << 12);
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">AUIPC x10, 0</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// Loads the current PC value into x10.</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                <div class="flex-col">
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Encoding</h3>
                        
                        <div class="bit-grid-container">
                            <div class="bit-grid-label">Binary Layout</div>
                            <div class="bit-row">
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="imm">
                                    <span class="bit-value">imm[31:12]</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rd">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rd</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="0010111">
                                    <span class="bit-value">0010111</span>
                                </div>
                                
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div class="meta-grid">
                            <div class="meta-item">
                                <span class="meta-label">Format</span>
                                <span class="badge">U-Type</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="meta-item">
                                <span class="meta-label">Opcode</span>
                                <span class="mono accent">0x17</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Operands</h3>
                        <ul class="operand-list" style="list-style: none;">
                            
                            <li class="operand-row" data-op="rd" style="padding: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); transition: background 0.2s; border-radius: 4px; padding-left: 8px;">
                                <span class="op-name" style="color: var(--accent); font-family: 'JetBrains Mono'; font-weight: bold;">rd</span>
                                <br>
                                <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted);">Dest</span>
                            </li>
                            
                            <li class="operand-row" data-op="imm" style="padding: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); transition: background 0.2s; border-radius: 4px; padding-left: 8px;">
                                <span class="op-name" style="color: var(--accent); font-family: 'JetBrains Mono'; font-weight: bold;">imm</span>
                                <br>
                                <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted);">20-bit offset</span>
                            </li>
                            
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>

            <h1 class="mono" style="font-size: 3rem; margin-top: 10px;">JAL</h1>
            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Jump and Link</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                JAL rd, offset
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Jumps to an offset and saves return address.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            R[rd] = PC + 4; PC += sext(offset);
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">JAL x1, 1024</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// Calls function at PC+1024, saves return address in RA (x1).</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                <div class="flex-col">
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Encoding</h3>
                        
                        <div class="bit-grid-container">

                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rd">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rd</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="1101111">
                                    <span class="bit-value">1101111</span>
                                </div>
                                
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div class="meta-grid">
                            <div class="meta-item">

                            </div>
                            <div class="meta-item">
                                <span class="meta-label">Opcode</span>
                                <span class="mono accent">0x6F</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Operands</h3>
                        <ul class="operand-list" style="list-style: none;">
                            
                            <li class="operand-row" data-op="rd" style="padding: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); transition: background 0.2s; border-radius: 4px; padding-left: 8px;">
                                <span class="op-name" style="color: var(--accent); font-family: 'JetBrains Mono'; font-weight: bold;">rd</span>

                                <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted);">Return Address Dest</span>

            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Add</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                ADD rd, rs1, rs2
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Adds the contents of two registers.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            R[rd] = R[rs1] + R[rs2];
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">ADD x6, x5, x4</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// x6 = x5 + x4</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rs1">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rs1</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="000">
                                    <span class="bit-value">000</span>
                                </div>

                                    <span class="bit-value">rd</span>
                                </div>

                                    <span class="bit-value">0110011</span>
                                </div>
                                
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                <span class="badge">R-Type</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="meta-item">
                                <span class="meta-label">Opcode</span>

            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Branch if Equal</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                BEQ rs1, rs2, offset
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Branches if two registers are equal.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            if (R[rs1] == R[rs2]) PC += sext(offset);
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">BEQ x5, x6, 100</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// Jump 100 bytes forward if x5 equals x6.</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                <div class="flex-col">
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Encoding</h3>
                        
                        <div class="bit-grid-container">
                            <div class="bit-grid-label">Binary Layout</div>
                            <div class="bit-row">
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="imm">
                                    <span class="bit-value">imm</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rs2">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rs2</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rs1">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rs1</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="000">
                                    <span class="bit-value">000</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="imm">
                                    <span class="bit-value">imm</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="1100011">
                                    <span class="bit-value">1100011</span>
                                </div>
                                
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div class="meta-grid">
                            <div class="meta-item">
                                <span class="meta-label">Format</span>
                                <span class="badge">B-Type</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="meta-item">
                                <span class="meta-label">Opcode</span>
                                <span class="mono accent">0x63</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Operands</h3>
                        <ul class="operand-list" style="list-style: none;">
                            
                            <li class="operand-row" data-op="rs1" style="padding: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); transition: background 0.2s; border-radius: 4px; padding-left: 8px;">
                                <span class="op-name" style="color: var(--accent); font-family: 'JetBrains Mono'; font-weight: bold;">rs1</span>
                                <br>
                                <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted);">Source 1</span>
                            </li>
                            
                            <li class="operand-row" data-op="rs2" style="padding: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); transition: background 0.2s; border-radius: 4px; padding-left: 8px;">
                                <span class="op-name" style="color: var(--accent); font-family: 'JetBrains Mono'; font-weight: bold;">rs2</span>
                                <br>
                                <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted);">Source 2</span>
                            </li>
                            
                            <li class="operand-row" data-op="offset" style="padding: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--border); transition: background 0.2s; border-radius: 4px; padding-left: 8px;">
                                <span class="op-name" style="color: var(--accent); font-family: 'JetBrains Mono'; font-weight: bold;">offset</span>
                                <br>
                                <span style="font-size: 0.85rem; color: var(--text-muted);">Branch target</span>
                            </li>
                            
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

            <h1 class="mono" style="font-size: 3rem; margin-top: 10px;">SW</h1>
            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Store Word</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                SW rs2, offset(rs1)
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Stores a 32-bit word to memory.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            M[R[rs1] + sext(offset)] = R[rs2][31:0];
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">SW x5, 12(x2)</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// Store x5 into stack memory at offset 12.</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                <div class="flex-col">
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Encoding</h3>
                        
                        <div class="bit-grid-container">
                            <div class="bit-grid-label">Binary Layout</div>
                            <div class="bit-row">
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="imm">
                                    <span class="bit-value">imm</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rs2">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rs2</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="rs1">
                                    <span class="bit-value">rs1</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="010">
                                    <span class="bit-value">010</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="imm">
                                    <span class="bit-value">imm</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="0100011">
                                    <span class="bit-value">0100011</span>
                                </div>
                                
                            </div>
                        </div>

            </div>

            </p>

                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">MOV RAX, RBX</div>

            <h1 class="mono" style="font-size: 3rem; margin-top: 10px;">SUB (extended)</h1>
            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Subtract (Extended Register)</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                SUB <Xd>, <Xn>, <Wm>, <extend> {#<amount>}
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Subtracts an optionally-extended register value.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            Xd = Xn - Extend(Wm, amount);
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">SUB X0, X1, W2, UXTW</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// Subtracts W2 (zero extended) from X1.</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                <div class="flex-col">
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Encoding</h3>
                        
                        <div class="bit-grid-container">
                            <div class="bit-grid-label">Binary Layout</div>
                            <div class="bit-row">
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="sf">
                                    <span class="bit-value">sf</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="0001011">
                                    <span class="bit-value">0001011</span>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="001">
                                    <span class="bit-value">001</span>
                                </div>

            <h1 class="mono" style="font-size: 3rem; margin-top: 10px;">STR (immediate)</h1>
            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Store Register (Immediate offset)</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                STR <Xt>, [<Xn>, #<simm>]
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Stores a word or doubleword to memory.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            Mem[Xn + simm] = Xt;
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">STR X0, [SP, #8]</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// Store X0 to StackPointer + 8.</p>
                    </div>

            <h1 class="mono" style="font-size: 3rem; margin-top: 10px;">ADD (shifted)</h1>
            <h2 style="font-weight: 400; color: var(--text-muted);">Add (Shifted Register)</h2>
            
            <div class="syntax-box">
                ADD <Xd>, <Xn>, <Xm>{, <shift> #<amount>}
            </div>

            <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; margin-bottom: 30px; color: var(--text-main);">
                Adds a register value and an optionally-shifted register value.
            </p>

            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 2fr 1fr; gap: 20px;">
                
                <div>
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Pseudocode Operation</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="border:none; padding:0; background: transparent;">
                            Xd = Xn + Shift(Xm, shift, amount);
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    
                    <div class="panel">
                        <h3>Example</h3>
                        <div class="code-block" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">ADD X0, X1, X2, LSL #2</div>
                        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--text-muted);">// X0 = X1 + (X2 << 2)</p>
                    </div>
                    
                </div>

                                    <span class="bit-value">Rm</span>

                                <div class="bit-box" data-op="imm6">
                                    <span class="bit-value">imm6</span>
                                </div>

                                    <span class="bit-value">Rn</span>
                                </div>

                                    <span class="bit-value">Rd</span>

FILE: ./docs/static/search.js
==================================================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');
    const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('search-results');
    let searchIndex = [];
    let selectedIndex = -1;

    // 1. Fetch Search Index
    try {
        const path = typeof SEARCH_INDEX_PATH !== 'undefined' ? SEARCH_INDEX_PATH : 'search.json';
        const response = await fetch(path);
        searchIndex = await response.json();
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Could not load search index:", error);
    }

    // 2. Search Logic
    if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
            selectedIndex = -1;
            
            if (query.length < 2) {
                resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }

            // Smart Search: Check if all query parts exist in label or summary
            const terms = query.split(" ");
            const results = searchIndex.filter(item => {
                const text = (item.label + " " + item.summary).toLowerCase();
                return terms.every(term => text.includes(term));
            });

            renderResults(results);
        });

        // 3. Keyboard Navigation
        searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            const items = resultsContainer.querySelectorAll('.search-result-item');
            if (items.length === 0) return;

            if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
                e.preventDefault();
                selectedIndex = (selectedIndex + 1) % items.length;
                updateSelection(items);
            } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
                e.preventDefault();
                selectedIndex = (selectedIndex - 1 + items.length) % items.length;
                updateSelection(items);
            } else if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (selectedIndex >= 0) {
                    items[selectedIndex].querySelector('a').click();
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function renderResults(results) {
        resultsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        if (results.length > 0) {
            resultsContainer.style.display = 'block';
            results.slice(0, 10).forEach((result, index) => {
                const div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'search-result-item';
                div.innerHTML = `
                    <a href="${typeof SEARCH_INDEX_PATH !== 'undefined' ? SEARCH_INDEX_PATH.replace('search.json', '') : './'}${result.url}">
                        <div class="result-title">${result.label}</div>
                        <div class="result-summary">${result.summary}</div>
                    </a>
                `;
                div.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                    selectedIndex = index;
                    updateSelection(resultsContainer.querySelectorAll('.search-result-item'));
                });
                resultsContainer.appendChild(div);
            });
        } else {
            resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }

    function updateSelection(items) {
        items.forEach((item, index) => {
            if (index === selectedIndex) {
                item.classList.add('selected');
                item.scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest' });
            } else {
                item.classList.remove('selected');
            }
        });
    }

    // Close on click outside
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (searchInput && !e.target.closest('.search-wrapper')) {
            resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
});

FILE: ./docs/static/theme.js

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
    const root = document.documentElement;
    const icon = toggleBtn.querySelector('span');

    // 1. Check Local Storage
    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme');
    if (savedTheme === 'light') {
        root.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
        icon.textContent = 'üåô'; // Moon icon for switching BACK to dark
    } else {
        icon.textContent = '‚òÄÔ∏è'; // Sun icon for switching TO light
    }

    // 2. Toggle Logic
    toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const currentTheme = root.getAttribute('data-theme');
        
        if (currentTheme === 'light') {
            // Switch to Dark
            root.removeAttribute('data-theme');
            localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
            icon.textContent = '‚òÄÔ∏è';
        } else {
            // Switch to Light
            root.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
            localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
            icon.textContent = 'üåô';
        }
    });
});

FILE: ./docs/static/animation.js
==================================================
const canvas = document.getElementById('hero-canvas');
const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

let width, height;
let particles = [];

function resize() {
    width = canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
    height = canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
}

class Particle {
    constructor() {
        this.x = Math.random() * width;
        this.y = Math.random() * height;
        this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
        this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
        this.size = Math.random() * 2;
    }
    update() {
        this.x += this.vx;
        this.y += this.vy;
        if (this.x < 0 || this.x > width) this.vx *= -1;
        if (this.y < 0 || this.y > height) this.vy *= -1;
    }
    draw() {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(56, 189, 248, 0.5)'; // Your accent color
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fill();
    }
}

function init() {
    particles = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < 50; i++) particles.push(new Particle());
}

function animate() {
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
    
    // Draw particles
    particles.forEach(p => {
        p.update();
        p.draw();
    });

    // Draw connections
    for (let i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
        for (let j = i; j < particles.length; j++) {
            const dx = particles[i].x - particles[j].x;
            const dy = particles[i].y - particles[j].y;
            const distance = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy);
            
            if (distance < 150) {
                ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(56, 189, 248, ${0.1 - distance/1500})`;
                ctx.lineWidth = 1;
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.moveTo(particles[i].x, particles[i].y);
                ctx.lineTo(particles[j].x, particles[j].y);
                ctx.stroke();
            }
        }
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(animate);
}

window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
resize();
init();
animate();

FILE: ./docs/static/interactions.js
==================================================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // 1. Interactive Bit-Field Highlighting
    const bitBoxes = document.querySelectorAll('.bit-box');
    const operandRows = document.querySelectorAll('.operand-row');

    function highlight(name, active) {
        // Find bit boxes with this name
        bitBoxes.forEach(box => {
            if (box.dataset.op === name) {
                if(active) box.classList.add('highlight');
                else box.classList.remove('highlight');
            }
        });

        // Find operand rows with this name
        operandRows.forEach(row => {
            if (row.dataset.op === name) {
                if(active) row.classList.add('highlight');
                else row.classList.remove('highlight');
            }
        });
    }

    // Attach events to Bit Boxes
    bitBoxes.forEach(box => {
        if(box.dataset.op) { // Only if it has a name
            box.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => highlight(box.dataset.op, true));
            box.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => highlight(box.dataset.op, false));
        }
    });

    // Attach events to Operand Rows
    operandRows.forEach(row => {
        if(row.dataset.op) {
            row.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => highlight(row.dataset.op, true));
            row.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => highlight(row.dataset.op, false));
        }
    });
});

<script>
    // Bridge the hero input to the main search logic if present
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        const heroInput = document.getElementById('hero-search');
        const heroResults = document.getElementById('hero-results');
        const mainInput = document.getElementById('search-input'); // The nav bar input
        
        // Hide nav bar input on homepage to avoid clutter
        if(mainInput && window.innerWidth > 768) {
             mainInput.closest('.search-wrapper').style.visibility = 'hidden';
        }

        // Reuse the logic by dispatching events or simple duplication
        // For simplicity in this mega-update, I'll let search.js handle the Nav one, 
        // and copy the minimal fetch logic here for the Hero one to ensure it works 100%
        
        let searchIndex = [];
        fetch('search.json')
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => searchIndex = data);

        heroInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
            heroResults.innerHTML = '';
            if (query.length < 2) { heroResults.style.display = 'none'; return; }

            const terms = query.split(" ");
            const results = searchIndex.filter(item => {
                const text = (item.label + " " + item.summary).toLowerCase();
                return terms.every(term => text.includes(term));
            });

            if (results.length > 0) {
                heroResults.style.display = 'block';
                results.slice(0, 8).forEach(result => {
                    const div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.className = 'search-result-item';
                    div.innerHTML = `<a href="${result.url}"><div class="result-title">${result.label}</div><div class="result-summary">${result.summary}</div></a>`;
                    heroResults.appendChild(div);
                });
            } else { heroResults.style.display = 'none'; }
        });
        
        // Keyboard shortcut focuses Hero input on Homepage
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'k') {
                e.preventDefault();
                heroInput.focus();
            }
        });
    });
</script>

FILE: ./static/search.js
==================================================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');
    const resultsContainer = document.getElementById('search-results');
    let searchIndex = [];
    let selectedIndex = -1;

    // 1. Fetch Search Index
    try {
        const path = typeof SEARCH_INDEX_PATH !== 'undefined' ? SEARCH_INDEX_PATH : 'search.json';
        const response = await fetch(path);
        searchIndex = await response.json();
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Could not load search index:", error);
    }

    // 2. Search Logic
    if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
            selectedIndex = -1;
            
            if (query.length < 2) {
                resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }

            // Smart Search: Check if all query parts exist in label or summary
            const terms = query.split(" ");
            const results = searchIndex.filter(item => {
                const text = (item.label + " " + item.summary).toLowerCase();
                return terms.every(term => text.includes(term));
            });

            renderResults(results);
        });

        // 3. Keyboard Navigation
        searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            const items = resultsContainer.querySelectorAll('.search-result-item');
            if (items.length === 0) return;

            if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
                e.preventDefault();
                selectedIndex = (selectedIndex + 1) % items.length;
                updateSelection(items);
            } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
                e.preventDefault();
                selectedIndex = (selectedIndex - 1 + items.length) % items.length;
                updateSelection(items);
            } else if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (selectedIndex >= 0) {
                    items[selectedIndex].querySelector('a').click();
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function renderResults(results) {
        resultsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        if (results.length > 0) {
            resultsContainer.style.display = 'block';
            results.slice(0, 10).forEach((result, index) => {
                const div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'search-result-item';
                div.innerHTML = `
                    <a href="${typeof SEARCH_INDEX_PATH !== 'undefined' ? SEARCH_INDEX_PATH.replace('search.json', '') : './'}${result.url}">
                        <div class="result-title">${result.label}</div>
                        <div class="result-summary">${result.summary}</div>
                    </a>
                `;
                div.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                    selectedIndex = index;
                    updateSelection(resultsContainer.querySelectorAll('.search-result-item'));
                });
                resultsContainer.appendChild(div);
            });
        } else {
            resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }

    function updateSelection(items) {
        items.forEach((item, index) => {
            if (index === selectedIndex) {
                item.classList.add('selected');
                item.scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest' });
            } else {
                item.classList.remove('selected');
            }
        });
    }

    // Close on click outside
    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (searchInput && !e.target.closest('.search-wrapper')) {
            resultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
});

FILE: ./static/theme.js
==================================================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
    const root = document.documentElement;
    const icon = toggleBtn.querySelector('span');

    // 1. Check Local Storage
    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme');
    if (savedTheme === 'light') {
        root.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
        icon.textContent = 'üåô'; // Moon icon for switching BACK to dark
    } else {
        icon.textContent = '‚òÄÔ∏è'; // Sun icon for switching TO light
    }

    // 2. Toggle Logic
    toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const currentTheme = root.getAttribute('data-theme');
        
        if (currentTheme === 'light') {
            // Switch to Dark
            root.removeAttribute('data-theme');
            localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
            icon.textContent = '‚òÄÔ∏è';
        } else {
            // Switch to Light
            root.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
            localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
            icon.textContent = 'üåô';
        }
    });
});


==================================================
FILE: ./static/animation.js
==================================================
const canvas = document.getElementById('hero-canvas');
const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

let width, height;
let particles = [];

function resize() {
    width = canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
    height = canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
}

class Particle {
    constructor() {
        this.x = Math.random() * width;
        this.y = Math.random() * height;
        this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
        this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
        this.size = Math.random() * 2;
    }
    update() {
        this.x += this.vx;
        this.y += this.vy;
        if (this.x < 0 || this.x > width) this.vx *= -1;
        if (this.y < 0 || this.y > height) this.vy *= -1;
    }
    draw() {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(56, 189, 248, 0.5)'; // Your accent color
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fill();
    }
}

function init() {
    particles = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < 50; i++) particles.push(new Particle());
}

function animate() {
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
    
    // Draw particles
    particles.forEach(p => {
        p.update();
        p.draw();
    });

    // Draw connections
    for (let i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
        for (let j = i; j < particles.length; j++) {
            const dx = particles[i].x - particles[j].x;
            const dy = particles[i].y - particles[j].y;
            const distance = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy);
            
            if (distance < 150) {
                ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(56, 189, 248, ${0.1 - distance/1500})`;
                ctx.lineWidth = 1;
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.moveTo(particles[i].x, particles[i].y);
                ctx.lineTo(particles[j].x, particles[j].y);
                ctx.stroke();
            }
        }
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(animate);
}

window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
resize();
init();
animate();


==================================================
FILE: ./static/interactions.js
==================================================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // 1. Interactive Bit-Field Highlighting
    const bitBoxes = document.querySelectorAll('.bit-box');
    const operandRows = document.querySelectorAll('.operand-row');

    function highlight(name, active) {
        // Find bit boxes with this name
        bitBoxes.forEach(box => {
            if (box.dataset.op === name) {
                if(active) box.classList.add('highlight');
                else box.classList.remove('highlight');
            }
        });

        // Find operand rows with this name
        operandRows.forEach(row => {
            if (row.dataset.op === name) {
                if(active) row.classList.add('highlight');
                else row.classList.remove('highlight');
            }
        });
    }

    // Attach events to Bit Boxes
    bitBoxes.forEach(box => {
        if(box.dataset.op) { // Only if it has a name
            box.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => highlight(box.dataset.op, true));
            box.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => highlight(box.dataset.op, false));
        }
    });

    // Attach events to Operand Rows
    operandRows.forEach(row => {
        if(row.dataset.op) {
            row.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => highlight(row.dataset.op, true));
            row.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => highlight(row.dataset.op, false));
        }
    });
});
